          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Sunday, March 13, 2016</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='https://4.bp.blogspot.com/--focJlhopAM/VuYRJFQ1XwI/AAAAAAAAG44/YCovEprH2IwCm4s9AmHXsAjqRvF5Kh6Wg/s320/sky.png' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='2449051083559529141' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='4269167788120608934' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='4269167788120608934'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://doginasweatermusicreviews.blogspot.com/2016/03/skylar-gudasz-oleander-daniel-13-2016.html'>Skylar Gudasz - Oleander (Daniel 13, 2016)</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-4269167788120608934' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/--focJlhopAM/VuYRJFQ1XwI/AAAAAAAAG44/YCovEprH2IwCm4s9AmHXsAjqRvF5Kh6Wg/s1600/sky.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" src="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/--focJlhopAM/VuYRJFQ1XwI/AAAAAAAAG44/YCovEprH2IwCm4s9AmHXsAjqRvF5Kh6Wg/s320/sky.png" width="320" /></a></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Skylar Gudasz</b></span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Oleander</b></span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Daniel 13</b></span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>2016</b></span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b><br /></b></span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Rating</b>: 7.5 made-for-TV-movies out of 10</span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Despite
 being local I know next to nothing about <a href="http://www.skylargudasz.com/"><b>Skylar Gudasz</b></a>.&nbsp; And because of
 that, it's easy for me to entertain the rumor (that I just completely made up) 
that this is actually a long lost Karen Carpenter record that Skylar found in 
an old dusty barn and decided to release under her own name. Yeah, 
there's probably a little bit more twang to this than you would expect 
from a Carpenter record, but maybe that's the direction she was heading 
in before the recordings got lost in that barn!&nbsp; I mean, it's possible 
right?</span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">According to this <a href="http://www.indyweek.com/indyweek/record-review-skylar-gudasz-owns-her-influences-with-the-brilliant-oleander/Content?oid=4996407">much better write-up</a> 
by my man Grayson, someone who is actually paid to give his opinion on 
music, Gudasz employed a "who's who" in creating "Oleander" - Chris Stamey
 (the dBs) recorded it, and she had musical assistance from a wide 
swath including the North Carolina Symphony, Django Haskins (Old 
Ceremony), Brad Cook (Megafaun), and even the one-and-only Norman Blake 
(Teenage Fanclub)!&nbsp; Her high-quality choices in musical accompaniment 
fall right in line with the high-quality of her songwriting - there is a
 timeless nature to her material...these songs (and by extension, her 
fantastic voice) feel like they've been around forever.&nbsp; Fans of Sharon 
Van Etten, Aimee Mann, and fellow locals Mount Moriah would be 
well served to pick this one up. &nbsp;</span></div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-footer'>

<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://doginasweatermusicreviews.blogspot.com/2016/03/mount-moriah-how-to-dance-merge-2016.html'>Mount Moriah - How To Dance (Merge, 2016)</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-8212771515175345541' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-4F35mz6OuC0/VuYMxwvGKuI/AAAAAAAAG4s/NQNn_Tp4-UMWhsQk4pli5VUnb0zetJ0SA/s1600/mount.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="275" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-4F35mz6OuC0/VuYMxwvGKuI/AAAAAAAAG4s/NQNn_Tp4-UMWhsQk4pli5VUnb0zetJ0SA/s320/mount.jpg" width="320" /></a></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Mount Moriah</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">How To Dance</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Merge</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">2016</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span></b></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Rating</b>: 7 cannery workers out of 10</span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">The
 third record from <a href="http://mountmoriahband.com/"><b>Mount Moriah</b></a>, and absolutely no drop off in quality -
 not a small feat considering how outstanding their self-titled debut was.&nbsp;
 That release is still my favorite, to be honest, but I'm not calling anyone
 to complain about "How To Dance" - hell, I'm such a fan I pre-ordered it
 months before it came out. &nbsp;</span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Nothing on this 
record is an instant gut punch like "Lament" from their debut, but 
opener "Calvander" is a damn fine effort.&nbsp; Heather's voice is as strong 
if not stronger than ever, and let's not kid ourselves that is the main 
draw of this band, at least for me (and I'm the stupid person writing this).&nbsp; If there is anything negative to be
 said at all, it's the lack of sparse songs ala "Plane" from their first
 record - very little instrumentation and Heather's voice doing the 
heavy lifting.&nbsp; Yeah that's a weird thing to fuss over, but I really dig
 that style.&nbsp; But the entire new record is a keeper, even if it is a 
hair more upbeat than I would prefer.&nbsp; I'm gonna listen to it a lot 
regardless.&nbsp; </span></div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-footer'>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Thursday, February 25, 2016</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-YKzfNtzX4Ns/Vs_d3Y28MaI/AAAAAAAAG4M/l4JzUROZMEc/s320/dan.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='2449051083559529141' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='1337144452713961242' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='1337144452713961242'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://doginasweatermusicreviews.blogspot.com/2016/02/dan-sartain-century-plaza-one-little.html'>Dan Sartain - Century Plaza (One Little Indian, 2016)</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-1337144452713961242' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-YKzfNtzX4Ns/Vs_d3Y28MaI/AAAAAAAAG4M/l4JzUROZMEc/s1600/dan.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" src="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-YKzfNtzX4Ns/Vs_d3Y28MaI/AAAAAAAAG4M/l4JzUROZMEc/s320/dan.jpg" width="320" /></a></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Dan Sartain</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Century Plaza</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">One Little Indian</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">2016</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span></b></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Rating</b>: 8 paddlin' belts out of 10</span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><a href="http://dansartain.com/"><b>Dan Sartain</b></a> has always been a garage rocker type of dude, recording and 
performing music that was ok but never got me overly excited.&nbsp; He's been
 around for nearly a couple of decades, releasing an album seemingly 
every year, and to be perfectly honest I stopped paying attention a long
 time ago.&nbsp; I honestly don't know how this new album "Century 
Plaza" even got on my computer, but I've had a lot more free time to 
listen to music this past month or so, so why not see what the hell Dan 
Sartain is up to these days?</span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Well, it ain't 
garage rock anymore.&nbsp; It appears that for at least this album, Sartain 
has re-invented himself as a new wave electro-pop artist writing dark, 
almost gothy songs that would make Depeche Mode, Gary Numan and
 Suicide all proud.&nbsp; The highlight is the album opener, a remake of his 
own song "Walk Among the Cobras" that would sound right at home on the 
"Drive" soundtrack.&nbsp; All of the sudden I'm a big Dan Sartain fan now because
 I absolutely love this.&nbsp; Keep going in this direction Dan!</span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span></div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-MP753iS-vdY/Vs_bmNdVgsI/AAAAAAAAG4A/5xALcsMb5gQ/s320/court.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='2449051083559529141' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='6205924449279369560' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='6205924449279369560'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://doginasweatermusicreviews.blogspot.com/2016/02/courtney-barnett-sometimes-i-sit-and.html'>Courtney Barnett - Sometimes I Sit and Think, and Sometimes I Just Sit (Mom + Pop, 2015)</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6205924449279369560' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-MP753iS-vdY/Vs_bmNdVgsI/AAAAAAAAG4A/5xALcsMb5gQ/s1600/court.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" src="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-MP753iS-vdY/Vs_bmNdVgsI/AAAAAAAAG4A/5xALcsMb5gQ/s320/court.jpg" width="320" /></a></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Courtney Barnett</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Sometimes I Sit and Think, and Sometimes I Just Sit</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Mom + Pop</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">2015</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span></b></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Rating</b>: 8 dinging ringers out of 10</span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><a href="http://socialhub.courtneybarnett.com.au/"><b>Courtney Barnett</b></a> is the extremely rare example where the tastemakers that decide
 who gets to be popular actually picked someone making really great 
music, and moreover really great music that I quite like.&nbsp; There are 
about a million reviews of this already so consider this "review" more 
of a "thumbs up popular media, you actually got one right!" &nbsp;Also, it's 
almost a year old at this point and nobody gives a shit.&nbsp; 
Additional thumbs up to Courtney's voice, because I love it when I can actually 
hear the accents of where they are from when they sing...or sorta 
sing-talk, in Courtney's case.&nbsp; Even more thumbs up for the production 
on this record - it sounds goddamn amazing.&nbsp; I'm totally out of thumbs now.&nbsp; </span></div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Friday, February 12, 2016</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ObthOL0faDI/Vr6iwgTm_NI/AAAAAAAAG3w/6LQtD3XSo9g/s320/benj.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='2449051083559529141' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='8197657322258478497' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='8197657322258478497'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://doginasweatermusicreviews.blogspot.com/2016/02/benji-hughes-songs-in-key-of-animals.html'>Benji Hughes - Songs in the Key of Animals (Merge, 2016)</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-8197657322258478497' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ObthOL0faDI/Vr6iwgTm_NI/AAAAAAAAG3w/6LQtD3XSo9g/s1600/benj.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" src="https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ObthOL0faDI/Vr6iwgTm_NI/AAAAAAAAG3w/6LQtD3XSo9g/s320/benj.jpg" width="320" /></a></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Benji Hughes</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Songs in the Key of Animals</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">Merge</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">2016</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></b></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><b>Rating</b>: 6.5 well-fed giraffes out of 10</span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">I
 have no idea what to make of this <a href="https://www.facebook.com/benjihughesofficial/"><b>Benji Hughes</b></a> record.&nbsp; He's from 
Charlotte so he's sort of a local, but despite playing live A LOT all over 
the Triangle over at least the last five years if not longer, I've never paid much attention.&nbsp; By all accounts he puts on a
 tremendous live show, so not seeing him after all of these years is probably a personal 
failing on my part.&nbsp; This record, "Songs in the Key of Animals," his 
first for Merge, is stylistically all over the map.&nbsp; He'll span from 
Parliment-like funk one song to a modern impression of Dr. John on the next song to 
something that sounds like an outtake from a National album after that.&nbsp;
 Thing is, he does a damn fine job of all of these different styles 
without any of them feeling like mimicry or he's ripping the original 
artists off.</span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;"><br /></span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">As interesting as this record is, 
I'm not sure how much I would actually listen to it just out of the 
blue.&nbsp; It's almost too all over the place, like a mixtape with no theme.&nbsp; But I definitely want to go see him live now, because there's no 
way these songs aren't fun</span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;">performed with a full band. &nbsp;</span></div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-footer'>
<div class='post-footer-line post-footer-line-1'>

<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-83r8iYapEic/Vr6eTUZ85_I/AAAAAAAAG3k/30euBfSim84/s320/bully.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='2449051083559529141' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='7110624734105710876' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='7110624734105710876'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://doginasweatermusicreviews.blogspot.com/2016/02/bully-feels-like-columbia-2015.html'>Bully - Feels Like (Columbia, 2015)</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7110624734105710876' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-83r8iYapEic/Vr6eTUZ85_I/AAAAAAAAG3k/30euBfSim84/s1600/bully.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="317" src="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-83r8iYapEic/Vr6eTUZ85_I/AAAAAAAAG3k/30euBfSim84/s320/bully.jpg" width="320" /></a></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Bully</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Feels Like</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Columbia</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">2015</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span></b></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Rating</b>: 7.5 old habits out of 10</span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">The
 sound of the nineties are alive and well with the new kids, and <a href="http://www.bullythemusic.com/"><b>Bully</b></a> 
are as good an example as any currently on the scene.&nbsp; I see lots of PJ Harvey comparisons, and
 maybe I hear that a little in the vocals, but musically I'm not there 
at all.&nbsp; I've even seen some Hole comparisons, which get a 
huge "hell no" from me (I never liked Hole so there's a lot of bias 
in that reaction).&nbsp; On Bully's best songs like "Milkman," "I Remember," 
and "Brainfreeze," the most apt comparison might be the driving indie 
punk guitars of Superchunk or the mid-nineties version of Dinosaur 
Jr (when it was really just J Mascis solo even though he still called it Dinosaur Jr.).&nbsp; Bully doesn't sound exactly 
like Speedy Ortiz, but both acts are mining the same territory musically
 - and for my money, Bully are doing it just a little bit better.&nbsp; I'll 
be honest, not nuts about their slower songs, but hopefully they grow on
 me.&nbsp; The upbeat tracks (such as those mentioned above) are so damn good
 it doesn't matter though, as this record is a keeper for sure.&nbsp; </span></div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-8ssFPBBZVOg/Vr6ZDWtXdSI/AAAAAAAAG3U/jhhlK2x0ZcQ/s1600/kurt.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='2449051083559529141' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='7753552492546763293' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='7753552492546763293'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://doginasweatermusicreviews.blogspot.com/2016/02/kurt-vile-blieve-im-goin-down-matador.html'>Kurt Vile - B'lieve I'm Goin Down... (Matador, 2015)</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7753552492546763293' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-8ssFPBBZVOg/Vr6ZDWtXdSI/AAAAAAAAG3U/jhhlK2x0ZcQ/s1600/kurt.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-8ssFPBBZVOg/Vr6ZDWtXdSI/AAAAAAAAG3U/jhhlK2x0ZcQ/s1600/kurt.jpg" /></a></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Kurt Vile&nbsp;</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">B'lieve I'm Goin Down...</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Matador</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">2015</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span></b></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Rating</b>: 7.5 giant chocolate chip cookies out of 10</span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">I
 often wonder if my brain would automatically think of <b><a href="http://www.kurtvile.com/">Kurt Vile</a></b> and War
 on Drugs at the same time if I didn't already know of their connection,
 because it's what I always get stuck in my head whether I like it or not.&nbsp; The War on Drugs 
went in more of a rock direction ala Tom Petty or Dire Straits, and Vile 
likes to hang out in the folkier/Bob Dylan-esque part of town - but the 
same vibe is there for me for both artists.&nbsp; I kinda feel like either act could cover the work of the other and make it feel like they were the original authors of 
the songs.&nbsp; Why does any of this matter?&nbsp; It doesn't, but my stupid 
brain was really stuck on this topic as I listened to "B'lieve I'm Goin Down...".&nbsp; </span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Long 
story short, this record is probably Vile's best work; 
"Pretty Pimpin'" is an amazing opener and the best song on the album; 
and I'd give anything to hear War on Drugs take Vile's folky songs and get real loud
 and stretchy with them like they do so well.&nbsp; </span></div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-14qwelvPvIo/Vr6XGtDV1mI/AAAAAAAAG3I/4Yf0XsgCw8g/s320/parq.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='2449051083559529141' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='5512899401630127367' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='5512899401630127367'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://doginasweatermusicreviews.blogspot.com/2016/02/parquet-courts-monastic-living-ep-rough.html'>Parquet Courts - Monastic Living EP (Rough Trade, 2015)</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-5512899401630127367' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-14qwelvPvIo/Vr6XGtDV1mI/AAAAAAAAG3I/4Yf0XsgCw8g/s1600/parq.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" src="https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-14qwelvPvIo/Vr6XGtDV1mI/AAAAAAAAG3I/4Yf0XsgCw8g/s320/parq.jpg" width="320" /></a></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Parquet Courts</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Monastic Living EP</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Rough Trade</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">2015</span></b></div>
<div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span></b></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Rating</b>: 5.5 coozy bottle openers out of 10</span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">I
 appreciate that <a href="https://parquetcourts.wordpress.com/"><b>Parquet Courts</b></a> got a wild hair and decided they would 
try to do a Devo imitation for this EP, but it instantly reminded me that I'd rather just listen to the real Devo.&nbsp; I suppose points to them for reminding me to listen to 
Devo, and that's not a bad thing.&nbsp; Everyone should listen to more Devo.&nbsp; </span></div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-footer'>
<div class='post-footer-line post-footer-line-1'>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Wednesday, January 13, 2016</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-FtoK_83jk5Y/Vl_daGLdFpI/AAAAAAAAGzY/YX-R868u4bk/s320/Mount%2BMoriah%2B-%2BCalvander.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='2449051083559529141' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='5085806929065967995' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='5085806929065967995'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://doginasweatermusicreviews.blogspot.com/2016/01/mount-moriah-calvander-7-merge-2015.html'>Mount Moriah - Calvander 7'' (Merge, 2015)</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-5085806929065967995' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-FtoK_83jk5Y/Vl_daGLdFpI/AAAAAAAAGzY/YX-R868u4bk/s1600/Mount%2BMoriah%2B-%2BCalvander.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-FtoK_83jk5Y/Vl_daGLdFpI/AAAAAAAAGzY/YX-R868u4bk/s320/Mount%2BMoriah%2B-%2BCalvander.jpg" width="320" /></a></span></div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Mount Moriah</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Calvander 7''</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Merge</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>2015</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b><br /></b></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Rating</b>: 7 bloody bags out of 10</span><br />
<br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">The last <a href="http://mountmoriahband.com/"><b>Mount Moriah</b></a> album "Miracle Temple" was still a pretty good effort, but I loved their self-titled debut so much and had such high expectations they really had nowhere to go but down.&nbsp; Happily, I like this new seven inch by them so much it re-ignited my excitement and I've already pre-ordered their next album that's coming out in the next month or two.&nbsp; The title track and the demo version of "Baby Blue" are both going to be on that next record, and both are totally great - a little twangy, a little dark, just the way I like their jams.&nbsp; The best track is the final one though, and the biggest reason to hunt this wax down -&nbsp; a live version of "Plane" from their self-titled effort.&nbsp; Probably my second favorite song of theirs ever, and the recording is resplendent.&nbsp; I'm real happy with this.&nbsp; </span>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Tuesday, January 12, 2016</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-E_Z5XrNerIY/VpW_AAzac6I/AAAAAAAAG1s/5i3NCV9EEFs/s320/royal_headache_high.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='2449051083559529141' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='6920226160769354698' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='6920226160769354698'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://doginasweatermusicreviews.blogspot.com/2016/01/royal-headache-high-whats-your-rupture.html'>Royal Headache - High (What's Your Rupture?, 2015)</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6920226160769354698' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-E_Z5XrNerIY/VpW_AAzac6I/AAAAAAAAG1s/5i3NCV9EEFs/s1600/royal_headache_high.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-E_Z5XrNerIY/VpW_AAzac6I/AAAAAAAAG1s/5i3NCV9EEFs/s320/royal_headache_high.jpg" width="320" /></a></div>
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Royal Headache</span></b><br />
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">High</span></b><br />
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">What's Your Rupture?</span></b><br />
<b><span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">2015</span></b><br />
<br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Rating</b>: 7.5 poor socialites out of 10</span><br />
<br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">I'm pretty sure I initially thought this release by <a href="http://royalheadache.com.au/"><b>Royal Headache</b></a> was Royal Baths, a band from San Francisco I saw live once that was kinda boring.&nbsp; Because of that, I didn't listen to this for ages, just sitting there on my computer collecting digital dust.&nbsp; Eventually I threw it on and...oh yeah, it's a totally different band and I'm an idiot.&nbsp; Every year there is at least one release that I listen to the shit out of the next year...my money is on "High" being very high on that list.</span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">The band's sound is a little all over the place, and don't really sound anything like the rest of the indie/punk crowd coming out of Australia these days.&nbsp; I suppose it is a big ass country and there would be no reason for things to be homogeneous to begin with, but it's easy to put other places in those nice neat boxes.&nbsp; More than anything they do a jangly pop-punk thing, but certainly not only that.&nbsp; The singer can get a little soulful, see "Wouldn't You Know";&nbsp; the band can sound like they are doing a Style Council cover, see "Need You", or perhaps Soul Asylum, see "Carolina"; and probably my favorite is the opener "My Own Fantasy," which would sound right at home on a Terry Malts album.&nbsp; The main thing that unites all these different influences is the band does all of them really well, and I'm already looking forward to listening to this record on repeat for a good chunk of 2016.&nbsp; </span>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Monday, December 21, 2015</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-I3zN97NcGsY/VnipEQHSMkI/AAAAAAAAG08/jkW02Y5tryM/s320/low.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='2449051083559529141' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='6029869680645097922' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='6029869680645097922'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://doginasweatermusicreviews.blogspot.com/2015/12/low-ones-and-sixes-sub-pop-2015.html'>Low - Ones and Sixes (Sub Pop, 2015)</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6029869680645097922' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-I3zN97NcGsY/VnipEQHSMkI/AAAAAAAAG08/jkW02Y5tryM/s1600/low.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-I3zN97NcGsY/VnipEQHSMkI/AAAAAAAAG08/jkW02Y5tryM/s320/low.jpg" width="320" /></a></span></div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Low</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Ones and Sixes</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Sub Pop</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>2015</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b><br /></b></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Rating</b>: 8 breathing snails out of 10</span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">I've long been a total fanboy of <a href="http://www.chairkickers.com/"><b>Low</b></a>, both in recorded form and live, ever since I randomly bought a used copy of "The Curtain Hits the Cast" in college...nearly twenty years ago.&nbsp; I don't feel good about typing that.&nbsp;&nbsp; I do, however, feel good about this new Low record "Ones and Sixes."&nbsp; There are never any great leaps or changes in what Low does - it's always subtle, and often takes a few listens to pinpoint.&nbsp; The two most noteworthy items on "Ones and Sixes" are the use of electronic drums to augment the simple drum beats that usually populate their tracks, and a strong Cocteau Twins vibe from the guitars on a few songs.&nbsp; Make no mistake though, any fan of Low is going to feel right at home with this one.&nbsp; As is always the case anytime they release a record, it's one of my favorites of the year.&nbsp; </span>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Thursday, December 17, 2015</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-erCE4nqZKMI/Vl_auxfEUOI/AAAAAAAAGzM/JaWwfdaFbH0/s320/Destroyer%2B-%2BPoyson%2BSeason.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='2449051083559529141' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='3336530879156579361' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='3336530879156579361'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://doginasweatermusicreviews.blogspot.com/2015/12/destroyer-poison-season-merge-2015.html'>Destroyer - Poison Season (Merge, 2015)</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-3336530879156579361' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-erCE4nqZKMI/Vl_auxfEUOI/AAAAAAAAGzM/JaWwfdaFbH0/s1600/Destroyer%2B-%2BPoyson%2BSeason.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-erCE4nqZKMI/Vl_auxfEUOI/AAAAAAAAGzM/JaWwfdaFbH0/s320/Destroyer%2B-%2BPoyson%2BSeason.jpg" width="320" /></a></span></div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Destroyer</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Poison Season</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Merge</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>2015</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b><br /></b></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Rating</b>: 8.5 male potency drugs out of 10</span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">It wasn't until I read another review that I realized this latest <a href="https://www.mergerecords.com/destroyer"><b>Destroyer</b></a> album, "Poison Season," carried a New York City theme throughout much of the songs.&nbsp; Listen, I hardly ever pay attention to lyrics - so long as they aren't super blatantly stupid, singers can pretty much be saying whatever they want.&nbsp; The thing is that musically, this album sounds very much like the late seventies in the greater New York City area - there are easy comparisons to Springsteen, Lou Reed and Bowie of that era.&nbsp; Not the vocals mind you - Dan Bejar sounds nothing like those three titans, but is amazing all the same on his own terms.&nbsp; The second track on the album, "Dream Lover," is instantly one of the top five best songs Destroyer has ever released - very strong praise in my opinion.&nbsp; I keep waiting for the inevitable downhill slide with Bejar and Destroyer, but album after album they not only meet but surpass my expectations.&nbsp; </span>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Monday, December 14, 2015</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-aAB1kAgof_c/Vm9-87Qj7sI/AAAAAAAAG0s/mRKYOOc63Yc/s320/arch.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='2449051083559529141' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='4368296276276044103' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='4368296276276044103'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://doginasweatermusicreviews.blogspot.com/2015/12/archers-of-loaf-curse-of-loaf-live-at.html'>Archers of Loaf - Curse of the Loaf - Live at Cat's Cradle (ARRA, 2015)</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-4368296276276044103' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-aAB1kAgof_c/Vm9-87Qj7sI/AAAAAAAAG0s/mRKYOOc63Yc/s1600/arch.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-aAB1kAgof_c/Vm9-87Qj7sI/AAAAAAAAG0s/mRKYOOc63Yc/s320/arch.jpg" width="320" /></a></div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Archers of Loaf</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Curse of the Loaf - Live at Cat's Cradle</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>ARRA</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>2015</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b><br /></b></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Rating</b>: vs. the Greatest of All Time</span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">As a self-professed superfan of the <a href="http://archersofloaf.net/"><b>Archers of Loaf</b></a>, the only thing that could possibly keep me from loving this is if the live recording was bad.&nbsp; It's not.&nbsp; I've seen them a good half-dozen times since their reformation, including one of the nights when this was recorded (August 19-20, 2011) if I remember correctly, and they give me that same excitement that they did when I saw them for the first time more than twenty years ago.&nbsp; No, a live recording isn't quite as good as the live experience, but it's still a damn fine representation of what is so great about this band.&nbsp; </span>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Thursday, November 5, 2015</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-D-a3cIgjb14/VjuHviC1q0I/AAAAAAAAGyo/K6upJbQbQQo/s320/cover.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='2449051083559529141' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='3311372403213306592' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='3311372403213306592'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://doginasweatermusicreviews.blogspot.com/2015/11/flesh-wounds-in-mouth-ep-snot-2015.html'>Flesh Wounds - In the Mouth EP (Snot, 2015)</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-3311372403213306592' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-D-a3cIgjb14/VjuHviC1q0I/AAAAAAAAGyo/K6upJbQbQQo/s1600/cover.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="320" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-D-a3cIgjb14/VjuHviC1q0I/AAAAAAAAGyo/K6upJbQbQQo/s320/cover.jpg" width="320" /></a></div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Flesh Wounds</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>In the Mouth EP</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Snot</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>2015</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b><br /></b></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Rating</b>: 8 political journals out of 10</span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">Running through six songs in about thirteen minutes, <a href="http://fleshwoundsband.com/"><b>Flesh Wounds</b></a> like to get right to the point.&nbsp; This is aggro old school-style punk that almost borders on hardcore at times.&nbsp; On the opener "Attack," it feels like you're being attacked for the entire 78 seconds of the song.&nbsp; This is a lot closer to early Black Flag or Negative Approach or the punk coming out of DC than it is the modern happy-go-lucky garage punk that the kids love so much.&nbsp; Most of the songs sound like singer Montgomery Morris is eating the microphone while he sings...I can attest after seeing them live a number of times that this is actually the case.&nbsp; As a side note, they have a song called "Joy Division Killed My Boner."</span>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-footer'>
<div class='post-footer-line post-footer-line-1'>

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Wednesday, November 4, 2015</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-o8e3TDNSc28/VjpXq1kYQPI/AAAAAAAAGyY/3LeINWr8cmU/s320/cas.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='2449051083559529141' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='5947321237009646951' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='5947321237009646951'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://doginasweatermusicreviews.blogspot.com/2015/11/caspian-dust-and-disquiet-triple-crown.html'>Caspian - Dust and Disquiet (Triple Crown, 2015)</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-5947321237009646951' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-o8e3TDNSc28/VjpXq1kYQPI/AAAAAAAAGyY/3LeINWr8cmU/s1600/cas.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="298" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-o8e3TDNSc28/VjpXq1kYQPI/AAAAAAAAGyY/3LeINWr8cmU/s320/cas.jpg" width="320" /></a></span></div>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Caspian</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Dust and Disquiet</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Triple Crown</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>2015</b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b><br /></b></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><b>Rating</b>: 7.5 headphone planets out of 10</span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;">I honest to god couldn't tell you much of anything that sets <a href="http://caspianmusic.net/"><b>Caspian</b></a> apart from Explosions in the Sky or Mono or This Will Destroy You or &lt;insert the name of other post-rock band here&gt;, but I can tell you it sounds totally fuckin' great.&nbsp; They do occasionally sing, and I mean very occasionally, so that's one small difference.&nbsp; Maybe a little more piano in their music?&nbsp; that's total speculation.&nbsp; They do the whole quiet-loud-quiet thing as well as anyone.&nbsp; I recently saw them perform live on the tour for this record, and it was outstanding.&nbsp; As with all of these bands, this is much better when listened to through headphones...jamming it through your car radio while cruising down the freeway, you're going to lose a lot of the nuance.&nbsp; This is definitely worth a listen though, regardless of format.&nbsp; </span>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-footer'>
